WRONG - solar energy will NEVER become more economical than traditional power sources of electricity - because it's not designed or intended to be.  There is not a single electrical engineer on the face of this planet that will tell you otherwise.  That's because the way how solar transference (how energy is created through a solar panel and turned into electricity) is "not designed" to be able to work with the current large electrical grid infrastructure to where it can contribute more than 15% of the total amount of power needed.  Even using home-solar systems to the max cannot create more than about 40% of the power needs for your own home - and that would mean have every square cm of your roof (if it's a big roof) covered with solar panels and most all of your front and rear yards (if you have them).  Of course, the size of the solar grid needed to transfer that much solar energy would be about the size of a RV - and where are you going to put that? (and it costs a fortune)  Again, go ask any electrical engineer.  I have a problem with all these "feel good" videos that simply skip over reality and absolute scientific fact!  My source:  I'm a licensed electrician and have installed numerous solar systems in both residential and commercial properties.  My suggestion:  convert everything to LNG and propane - it will easily achieve all the goals of the Paris Accord within ten years, and by the time all the LNG resources run out they should have hydrogen plant facilities perfected, as well as hydrogen fuel cell vehicles.  THAT is the future.

Oswald had supposedly fired his shots from the 6th floor,  then ran down unobserved by anyone to the 2nd floor he was first seen in those 90 seconds. The Warren Commission simply deleted the Coke Oswald was drinking from its published report.
